 nae naagarikta kanoon main pakistan, bangladesh or afghanistan ke gaiyr muslim utpeedit alpsankhyakon ko naagarikta dene kaa praavdhaan he
 Jeremy Lawrence, spokesman for the United Nations human rights body, said in Geneva, 'we are concerned about India's new Citizenship (amendment) Act 2019, the nature of which is fundamentally discriminatory
 'unhone kaha, 'sanshodhit kanoon bharat ke samvidhan main nihit kanoon ke samaksh samanta kii patibaddhta ko or antarashtriya naagarik evam raajnneetik adhikaar niyam tathaa nasleey bhedbhaav unmoolan sandhi main bharat ke dayitvon ko kamatar karata dikhataa he, jinamein bharat ek paksh he jo nasl, jati yaa dharmik aadhaar par bhedbhaav karne kii manaahi karata he
 The Foreign Ministry in Delhi had said that the new law calls for swift consideration for granting Indian citizenship to the oppressed religious minorities of some neighboring countries already living in India
 mantralay ne kaha tha ki prayek desh ko vibhinn nitiyon ke jariye apane nagarikon ko satyapit karne or gananaa karne kaa adhikaar he
 Lawrence said that there are still widespread laws granting citizenship in India, but these amendments would have a discriminatory effect on people seeking citizenship
 unhone kaha ki pravaas kii sthiti ko dekhe bina, sabhi pravasi sammaan, sangrakshan or apane maanavadhikaron kii purti ke hakdaar hai
